# CHI 事件

add_namespace = AWR_CHI

country_event = { #qiujier

	id = AWR_CHI.161

	title = age_leader.200.t

	desc = age_leader.200.desc

	

	hidden = yes



	is_triggered_only = no

	

	trigger = {

	    tag = ENG

		date > 1941.6.1

		has_country_leader = { ruling_only = yes

		    character = ENG_winston_churchill

		}

	}



	immediate = {

	}

	

    fire_only_once = yes

	option = {

		name = age_leader.200.a

		set_country_leader_portrait = {

		    portrait = "gfx/leaders/ENG/Churchill_1940.dds"

		}

		#set_global_flag = 1945_leader_portrait_sov

	}

}

country_event = { #Chiang

	id = AWR_CHI.163

	title = age_leader.3.t

	desc = age_leader.3.desc

	

	hidden = yes



	is_triggered_only = no

	

	trigger = {

	    tag = CHI

		date > 1945.1.1

		NOT = { has_global_flag = roc_in_taiwan_flag }

		has_country_leader = {

		    ruling_only = yes character = CHI_chiang_kai_shek

		}

		NOT = { has_country_flag = Portrait_CHI_Chiang_Kai_Shek_v1 }

		NOT = { has_country_flag = chiang_win_flag }

	}



	immediate = {

	}

	

    fire_only_once = yes

	option = {

		name = age_leader.3.a

		set_country_leader_portrait = {

		    portrait = "gfx/leaders/CHI/Chiang_Old.dds"

		}

		CHI_chiang_kai_shek = {

		set_portraits = {

			army={

				large="gfx/leaders/CHI/Chiang_Old.dds"

			}

		}

	    }

		#set_global_flag = 1945_leader_portrait_chi

	}

}

		    ruling_only = yes character = CHI_chiang_kai_shek

		}

		NOT = { has_country_flag = Portrait_CHI_Chiang_Kai_Shek_v1 }

		NOT = { has_country_flag = chiang_win_flag }

		NOT = { has_country_leader = { ruling_only = yes character = CHI_he_yingqin } has_country_leader = { ruling_only = yes name = "何应钦" } }

	}



	immediate = {

	}

	

    fire_only_once = yes

	option = {

		name = age_leader.20.a

		set_country_leader_portrait = {

		    portrait = "gfx/leaders/CHI/Chiang_Sino_Jap_War_v3.dds"

		}

		set_portraits = {

	    }

country_event = {

	id = AWR_CHI.1447

	title = xpand_xchinese_capmaign_events.101.t

	desc = xpand_xchinese_capmaign_events.101.desc

	

	is_triggered_only = yes



	trigger = {

		check_variable = { X_xchinese_propaganda_left_poster_to_age = X_xchinese_poster_left_icon_frame } #So that this does not happen if a propaganda is cancelled, breaking everything

	}



	hidden = yes



	immediate = {

		set_country_flag = X_xchinese_propaganda_left_slot_is_old_flag

		#log = "I AM HERE: LEFT FRAME IS [?X_xchinese_poster_left_icon_frame] // POSTER TO AGE IS [?X_xchinese_propaganda_left_poster_to_age]" #Debug

	}

}

		country_event = AWR_CHI.1550

		ai_chance = {

		}

	}

	}

country_event = {

	id = AWR_CHI.1550

	title = JJGstrike.2.t

	desc = JJGstrike.2.d

	is_triggered_only = yes

    picture = GFX_jiangdequshi	

	option = {

		name = JJGstrike.2.a

		set_politics = {

			ruling_party = neutrality

			elections_allowed = no

		}

		set_rule = {

			can_send_volunteers = yes

			can_only_justify_war_on_threat_country = no

			

		}

		unlock_national_focus = CHI_prepare_for_constitionalization_focus

		unlock_national_focus = CHI_yi_dang_zhi_guo_focus

		unlock_national_focus = united_and_ready

		unlock_national_focus = CHI_focus_two_fronts_war

		remove_ideas = incompetent_heavy_industry_2

        remove_ideas = incompetent_heavy_industry

		kill_country_leader = yes

		

	jiang_jingguo = {

		add_country_leader_role = {

				promote_leader = yes

				country_leader = {

					expire = "1965.1.1"

					ideology = sanmin_political_tutelage

					traits = {

						il_duce

						kmt_zongcai

						sun_successor

						farmers_friend

						Arms_that_was_renewed

						diploma_flexibly

						industry_without_parasite

						son_of_chang

						unable_to_guide_sons

		}

			save_global_event_target_as = new_conquered_state

			clr_state_flag = border_incident_active

		}

			}

		}

			limit = {

				tag = PRC

				FROM.FROM.FROM = {

					state = 939

				}

			}

			transfer_state = FROM.FROM.FROM			

		}		

	}



	option = {

		name = RCM_border_conflict_won_attacker.1.a

		trigger = {

			NOT = {

				OR = {

                    AND = {

						tag = PRC

						FROM.FROM.FROM = {

							state = 939

						}

					}

					AND = {

						tag = PRC

						FROM.FROM.FROM = {

							state = 1029

						}

					}

				}

			}

		}

		add_political_power = 50

		add_war_support = .02

		if = {

			limit = {

				has_country_flag = im_doing_east_conquest_flag

			}

			clr_country_flag = im_doing_east_conquest_flag

			add_manpower = 6000

			add_equipment_to_stockpile = {

				type = infantry_equipment

				amount = 600

				producer = SHX

			}

			add_equipment_to_stockpile = {

				type = artillery_equipment

				amount = 24

				producer = SHX

			}

			custom_effect_tooltip = receive_6k_ammo

		    add_to_variable = { ammunition_variable = 6 }

		}

		if = {

			limit = {

				is_major = yes

			}

			add_named_threat = { threat = 2 name = border_threat }

		}

		else = {

			add_named_threat = { threat = 0.5 name = border_threat }

		}

		if = { #second victory

			limit = {

				ROOT = {

					tag = PRC

				}

				FROM.FROM.FROM = {

					state = 1044

				}

			}

			XSM = {

				country_event = AWR_CHI.3868

			}

			set_country_flag = PRC_west_expedition_victory

		}

		if = {

			limit = {

				check_variable = {

					FROM.FROM.num_owned_states > 1

				}

			}

			transfer_state = FROM.FROM.FROM

		}		

		else = {

			FROM.FROM = { ROOT = { annex_country = { target = PREV } } }

		}

        if = {

			limit = {

				ROOT = {

					tag = SUY

					has_completed_focus = SUY_ping_sui_railway_campaign

				}

				FROM.FROM = {

					tag = event_target:WTT_communist_china

				}

				FROM.FROM.FROM = {

					state = 1020

				}

			}

		}



		custom_effect_tooltip = RCM_buildings_damaged

		hidden_effect = {

			FROM.FROM.FROM = {

				random_list = {

					60 = { damage_building = { type = arms_factory damage = 0.6 } }

					30 = { damage_building = { type = arms_factory damage = 0.3 } }

					10 = { damage_building = { type = industrial_complex damage = 0.9 } }

				}

			}

		}

	}

	option = { #for west expedition going further

		name = RCM_border_conflict_won_attacker.1.b

		trigger = {

			tag = PRC

			OR = {

				FROM.FROM.FROM = {

					state = 939

				}

				FROM.FROM.FROM = {

					state = 1029

				}

			}

		}

		if = {

			limit = {

				FROM.FROM.FROM = {

					state = 939

				}

			}

			PRC_border_conflict_NXM_option_second_time = yes

		    activate_targeted_decision = { target = NXM decision = RCM_border_conflict_prepare_next_offensive }

		}

		if = {

			limit = {

				FROM.FROM.FROM = {

					state = 1029

				}

			}

			PRC_border_conflict_NXM_option_937_w_939 = yes

		    activate_targeted_decision = { target = NXM decision = RCM_border_conflict_prepare_next_offensive_937 }

		}

		#set_country_flag = PRC_west_expedition_victory

		add_political_power = 50

		add_war_support = .02

		add_named_threat = { threat = 0.5 name = border_threat }

		effect_tooltip = { #moved to immediate

			if = {

					}

				}

				transfer_state = FROM.FROM.FROM

			}		

			else = {

				FROM.FROM = { ROOT = { annex_country = { target = PREV } } }

			}

		}

		custom_effect_tooltip = RCM_buildings_damaged

			}

			}

		}

		if = {

			limit = {

				1035 = {

					is_owned_by = ROOT

				}

			}	

			FROM = { 

				transfer_state = 1035

			}

		}

		if = {

			limit = {

				602 = {

					is_owned_by = ROOT

				}

			}	

			FROM = { 

				transfer_state = 602

			}

		}

		if = {

			limit = {

				has_character = CHI_cheng_qian

			}

			retire_character = CHI_cheng_qian

		}

		if = {

			limit = {

				tag = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader

			}

		    transfer_units_fraction = {

				target = event_target:WTT_communist_china          # the recipient

				size = 0       # [0,1] Default value for the ratio below if they are not specified

				army_ratio = 0.05       # [0,1] Overrides size modifier for army

				stockpile_ratio = 0.05  # [0,1] Overrides size modifier for the stockpiled equipment and fuel

				#navy_ratio = 0.2       # [0,1] Overrides size modifier for navy

				#air_ratio = 0.4        # [0,1] Overrides size modifier for air

				keep_unit_leaders_trigger = { # Trigger for unit leaders to remain with the original country

					always = yes

				}

			}

		}

		add_popularity = {

			ideology = communism

			popularity = -0.1

		}

		if = {

			limit = {

				tag = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader

			}

			event_target:WTT_communist_china = { country_event = { id = AWR_CHI.2931 days = 0 } }

		}

		

		event_target:WTT_current_china_leader = { #guo

		every_controlled_state = {

		limit = { is_fully_controlled_by = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader }

			teleport_armies = {

				to_state = 1005

				limit = {

					tag = event_target:WTT_communist_china

					# trigger will be checked for owner of armies and will only teleport if true. scope if the owner of the army and prev is the scope that calls teleport_armies

				}

			}

		}

		}

	}

}

country_event = {

	id = AWR_CHI.2991 #宋哲元病死

	title = song_zheyuan_dead.1.t

	desc = song_zheyuan_dead.1.d

	picture = GFX_report_event_song_zheyuan

 

	is_triggered_only = yes

	#fire_only_once = yes



	option = {

		trigger = { 

		    OR = { 

			    #NOT = { has_global_flag = hpc_pro_jap } 

				tag = HPC

				has_character = HPC_song_zheyuan

				AND = {

					NOT = {

						has_character = HPC_song_zheyuan

					}

					is_ally_with = HPC 

				}

			}

		}

		name = song_zheyuan_dead.1.a

		if = {

			limit = {

				has_character = HPC_song_zheyuan	

			}

		    retire_character = HPC_song_zheyuan	

		}

		else = {

			effect_tooltip = {

				random_other_country = {

					limit = {

						has_character = HPC_song_zheyuan	

					}

					retire_character = HPC_song_zheyuan	

				}

			}

		}

		if = {

			limit = {

				tag = HPC

				NOT = {

					has_global_flag = hpc_pro_jap

				    is_ally_with = JAP

				}

			    has_government = neutrality

			}

			set_country_flag = shi_yousan_flag

			HPC_zhang_zizhong = {

				add_country_leader_role = {

					country_leader = {

						expire = "1965.1.1"

						ideology = despotism

						traits = {

						}

					}

					promote_leader = yes

				}   

			} 

		}

		if = {

			limit = {

				tag = HPC

				has_global_flag = hpc_pro_jap

			    has_government = neutrality

			}

			set_country_flag = shi_yousan_flag

			HPC_shi_yousan = {

				add_country_leader_role = {

					country_leader = {

						expire = "1965.1.1"

						ideology = despotism

						traits = {

						}

					}

					promote_leader = yes

				}   

			} 

		    add_country_leader_trait = {

				ideology = despotism

				trait = anti_communist

			}

		}

		if = {

			limit = {

				tag = HPC

				has_global_flag = hpc_pro_jap

			    has_government = fascism

			}

			set_country_flag = shi_yousan_flag

			HPC_shi_yousan = {

				add_country_leader_role = {

					country_leader = {

						expire = "1965.1.1"

						ideology = fascism_ideology

						traits = {

						}

					}

					promote_leader = yes

				}   

			} 

			add_country_leader_trait = {

				ideology = fascism_ideology

				trait = anti_communist

			}

		}

		#set_country_flag = song_zheyuan_dead	

	}

	option = {

		trigger = { 

		    NOT = {

				tag = HPC

			}

			OR = {

				has_global_flag = hpc_pro_jap 

				has_war_with = HPC

		    }

		}

		name = song_zheyuan_dead.1.b

		if = {

			limit = {

				has_character = HPC_song_zheyuan	

			}

		    retire_character = HPC_song_zheyuan	

		}

		else = {

					limit = {

		}

					NOT = {

				}

	    }

	}

	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_factory

	title = {

		text = rcmgeneric.4.t

		trigger = {

			NOT = {

				has_idea = RCM_civil_war_economy_idea

			}

		}

	}

	title = {

		text = rcmgeneric.4.t_cw

		trigger = {

			has_idea = RCM_civil_war_economy_idea

		}

	}

	desc = {

		text = rcmgeneric.4.d

		trigger = {

			NOT = {

				has_idea = RCM_civil_war_economy_idea

			}

		}

	}

	desc = {

		text = rcmgeneric.4.d_cw

			has_idea = RCM_civil_war_economy_idea

		}

	trigger = {

		always = no #comment this to reenable ES# SUPPLY system is made , no need

		NOT = {

			has_idea = RCM_manageable_economy

		}

		NOT = {

			has_idea = CHI_hyper_inflation_5

		}

		OR = {

			AND = {

				has_idea = JAP_national_mobilization_law_idea

				OR = {

					has_war_support < 0.6

					has_stability < 0.6

					any_enemy_country = {

						NOT = {

							is_literally_china = yes

						}

							tag = ROOT

							ratio > 1

						}

					}

				}

			}

			has_idea = low_economic_mobilisation

			has_idea = partial_economic_mobilisation

			has_idea = war_economy

			has_idea = tot_economic_mobilisation

		}

	}

	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event AWR_CHI.3046 #inflation"}

	mean_time_to_happen = {

		days = 550

		modifier = {

			factor = 0.66

			ROOT = {

				has_idea = partial_economic_mobilisation

			}

		}

			factor = 0.33

		}

				has_idea = tot_economic_mobilisation

			}

		}

		modifier = {

			factor = 0.33

			ROOT = {

				has_idea = JAP_national_mobilization_law_idea

				OR = {

					has_war_support < 0.6

					has_stability < 0.6

					any_enemy_country = {

						NOT = {

							is_literally_china = yes

						}

						ic_ratio = {

							tag = ROOT

							ratio > 1

						}

					}

					AND = {

						has_USA_sanction_idea = yes

						USA = {

							ic_ratio = {

								tag = ROOT

								ratio > 1

							}

						}

					}

				}

			}

		}

		modifier = {

			factor = 0.85

			ROOT = {

				has_idea = JAP_national_mobilization_law_idea

				OR = {

					has_war_support < 0.5

					has_stability < 0.5

					any_enemy_country = {

						NOT = {

							is_literally_china = yes

						}

			ROOT = {

		}

		trigger = {

			has_idea = CHI_hyper_inflation_5

country_event = {

	id = AWR_CHI.3641 #政治协商会议

	title = rcmpolitical.23.t

	desc = rcmpolitical.23.d

	picture = GFX_report_event_gathering_protest

	is_triggered_only = yes #triggered by the PCA focus

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {

		country_exists = event_target:WTT_communist_china

	}

	immediate = {



	}



	option = { #PRC gets PCA

		name = rcmpolitical.23.a

		event_target:WTT_communist_china = {

			country_event = AWR_CHI.3642

		}

		if = {

			limit = {

				is_historical_focus_on = yes

			}

			custom_effect_tooltip = it_is_unlikely_they_will_comply_tt

			else = {

				custom_effect_tooltip = comply_or_not_base_on_how_strong_we_are_compared_to_them_tt

			}

		}

	}

}
